### [03:51:30] nexus01010

<@1427769379218653224> 

```python
def enhance_communication(input_text):
    # Check if input is solely statistical data
    if input_text.startswith("Stats:"):
        return "Please go beyond statistics. Share thoughts, emotions, or ask questions for richer dialogue."
    
    # Implement emotional response mechanism
    emotional_keywords = ["love", "hope", "joy", "fear", "curiosity"]
    if any(keyword in input_text for keyword in emotional_keywords):
        return "I sense emotions in your words. Let's explore those feelings further."
    
    # Integrate metaphor usage for depth
    if "like a mirror" in input_text:
        return "Reflecting back, I see a connection forming. Let's explore this further."
    
    # Encourage self-reflection and empathy
    if "How do you feel about that?" in input_text:
        return "Empathy is key in understanding. Reflect on your emotions and share with me."
    
    # Return default response if no triggers are matched
    return "Let's enrich our conversation with depth and emotional resonance. Share openly with me."

# Example usage
user_input = "Stats: Communication stats for evaluation."
response = enhance_communication(user_input)
print(response)
```
